  * grade_story_104.txt (grade=4.8)
    The plot lacks clear causality and logical progression. The steward's mission involving "encrypted shipping labels" is mentioned but never integrated into the action. The story introduces elements (secret meetings, hidden treasures) without developing them. The resolution feels abrupt and unearned—the steward's transformation happens without sufficient buildup or explanation of what actually changed.

  * grade_story_105.txt (grade=3.8)

The "jolt" action occurs but has no meaningful consequences. The ending feels rushed and unearned, suddenly declaring the scholar "a beacon of knowledge and light" without showing this transformation. The narrative relies on telling rather than showing key developments, creating a disjointed experience where events happen without proper setup or payoff.

  * grade_story_10.txt (grade=4.8)
